However, the hardware, design, and cheap feeling in the room make me feel that this hotel is more suitable for Orange Crystal or All Seasons. The brand vitality brought by Indigo, the hotel's just-right service, and the delicious breakfast pot stickers cannot change the cheap feeling of the room. I want to praise it as a small and beautiful place, but I can't praise it. Facilities: Indigo brand does not have a bathtub, which is acceptable. Let me say the good things first: Dyson hair dryer is standard, the bed and pillow are very comfortable, and if it were not for the poor sound insulation, I would sleep better. Other than that, it's all cheap goods. The door does not have a door stopper. The TV of the new hotel opened in 22 years cannot be projected. There is no smart toilet in the room, but there is a smart toilet in the lobby bathroom. It's beautiful on the outside, and there is no preferential trea**ent for guests who pay to stay. The sound insulation is at the express level. I was woken up by someone in the corridor while lying on the bed in the morning. The conversation between the guests and the waiter in the corridor can be heard clearly. The fabric wrapping at the bottom of the bed is fixed with staples. The staples in the room I stayed in were curled up, and I found it when my foot stepped on it and was stabbed.
The guest bathroom sink has no place to put soap and is not equipped with hand sanitizer 
The floor of the bedroom and the washing area is not leveled 

The hotel has only one restaurant, and the seats are not enough to cope with the May Day holiday. You have to queue up for meals in the morning, but the pot stickers and noodles are delicious üòã I like the pot stickers chef. Although the noodle guy is serious, he has great skills. It is the best pot stickers and noodles I have eaten in 2024

Service:
There was a small episode with an order when checking in, which was solved by the front desk 
This hotel does not seem to have a concierge. The front desk can also recommend fun places around 
The security guards in the driveway at the door and the security guards in the underground garage will take the initiative to greet and help guide and open the car door 
This hardware is not worthy of this service

Welcome fruit upon check-in: There are fruits but no knives and forks
Mini bar drinks: the first round of free drinks every day

I booked it after seeing the hotel ranked first on the Hangzhou design sense list
"Lobby" and B1 have a total of three designed locations for taking pictures. The design inside the room is almost a minus point
Design is not a simple stacking of elements, but to solve problems. From my room, the problem has not been solved At least it's not an Indigo-level room

Finally, I'll quote a passage from a TV that can't cast a screen and plays it in a loop
"Indigo is the face, and convenience is the substance"
